# Fuzzing Triage Report

## Crash analysis
No crash was observed in this campaign. Three factors most plausibly explain the null result. First, beacon frames transmitted by a non-AP STA are typically discarded by an AP-mode target at the MAC-filter or early parser stage without reaching deep IE processing, so the 2700 beacon variants provide weak signal regardless of mutation. Second, the len_overflow mutation is structurally inert in this campaign: for all three families the reported frame length is identical to the corresponding baseline, meaning IE-internal length inflation is bounded by total MPDU size and absorbed by the first bounds-check in the driver stack before any vulnerable parsing code is reached. Third, the authentication and assoc_request parsers on an AP-mode target are hardened rejection paths for unassociated STAs; the current IE-layer mutations (dup_ie, missing_mandatory, reserved_ie, oversized_value) exercise frame-body structure but do not reach fixed-field or state-machine code that is more likely to contain memory-safety bugs. The complete absence of probe_request frames and stateful sequences means the highest-value pre-association attack surface has not been probed at all.

## Findings
- [info] global/no_crash: All 8093 frames returned alive=1. No crash or DoS was induced across 3 frame families (beacon, authentication, assoc_request) over 6 mutation types and approximately 450 replay cycles per unique frame.
- [info] beacon/len_overflow: beacon/len_overflow reports len=101, identical to beacon/baseline len=101. The mutation inflates IE-internal length fields without growing the frame, so any declared overrun is bounded by total MPDU size and is likely caught by the first driver-level length check before deeper parsing.
- [info] authentication/len_overflow: authentication/len_overflow reports len=48, identical to authentication/baseline len=48. The Open System baseline (algorithm=0) carries no IEs at all per spec, so an IE-internal length overflow has nothing to act on; the mutation is a no-op for this configuration.
- [info] assoc_request/len_overflow: assoc_request/len_overflow reports len=80, identical to assoc_request/baseline len=80. IE length inflation without frame growth likely fails to trigger any OOB read condition in RSN (ID 48) or Extended Capabilities (ID 127) parsing.
- [anomaly] probe_request/entirely_absent: The probe_request frame family (management subtype 4) appears nowhere in the corpus despite being fully described in the spec notes. Probe Requests are processed pre-association and exercise a distinct scanning-state parser path that beacon, authentication, and assoc_request frames never reach. This is the largest unexplored attack surface in the current campaign.
- [anomaly] authentication/fixed_fields_untested: Authentication frames carry three 2-byte fixed fields (Algorithm Number, Transaction Sequence, Status Code) that are not targeted by any current mutation. Algorithm=0xFFFF (unknown), algorithm=1 (Shared Key) with wrong sequence number, or algorithm=3 (SAE) with Open-System-only frame body could expose state-machine handling bugs unreachable via the current IE-layer mutations.
- [info] beacon/fixed_fields_untested: Beacon's 12-byte fixed header (Timestamp 8 B, Beacon Interval 2 B, Capability Info 2 B) is untouched by all current mutations. Extreme Beacon Interval values (0x0000, 0xFFFF) and invalid Capability combinations may expose timing or mode-switching edge cases in beacon ingestion code.
- [anomaly] corpus/no_stateful_sequences: Every frame is replayed in isolation without building 802.11 association state. State-machine bugs such as accepting assoc_request without prior authentication, processing double-authentication, or injecting deauthentication mid-handshake are entirely untested by the current flat corpus structure.

## Next plan
{
  "focus_frames": [
    "probe_request",
    "authentication",
    "assoc_request"
  ],
  "focus_mutations": [
    "oversized_value",
    "dup_ie",
    "missing_mandatory",
    "fixed_field_corrupt",
    "truncated"
  ],
  "drop_frames": [
    "beacon"
  ],
  "rationale": "Beacon coverage is saturated at ~450 replays with zero signal; AP-mode targets discard foreign beacons before deep parsing and continuing to fuzz beacons wastes replay budget with no realistic crash path. probe_request must be added immediately as it is completely absent yet exposes a distinct pre-association scanning-state parser. For authentication, a new fixed_field_corrupt mutation targeting the Algorithm Number (values 0xFFFF, 1, 3), Transaction Sequence (out-of-order values), and Status Code fields should be prioritized because state-machine mishandling at the fixed-field layer is a common embedded driver bug class unreachable via IE mutations alone. A truncated mutation (genuine frame truncation to fewer bytes than the fixed-field or IE minimum) should complement len_overflow, which currently leaves total frame length unchanged and therefore cannot trigger read-past-end conditions gated on frame size. oversized_value and dup_ie remain worth retaining on authentication and assoc_request where they showed no effect in isolation but have never been applied within a stateful sequence (valid auth exchange followed immediately by a mutated assoc_request), which is the scenario most likely to expose parser assumptions about prior state."
}

## Raw campaign summary
Total frames replayed: 8093
Frame families exercised: assoc_request=2694, authentication=2699, beacon=2700
Mutations exercised: baseline=1349, dup_ie=1349, len_overflow=1349, missing_mandatory=1349, oversized_value=1349, reserved_ie=1348
No crash observed (target stayed alive for all frames).
